***охнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:охнуть.html>о́хнуть</a> (11301)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охать.html>о́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охнуть.html>о́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">óxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охать.html>о́хать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sigh, to moan</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">о́ханье</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">óxanʹje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ох.html>ох</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ox</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***охота.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́та</a> (1646)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хоте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xotétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oxóta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wish, inclination, desire</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охотник.html>охо́тник</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oxótnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">фотоохота</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">fotooxota</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охотничий.html>охо́тничий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oxótničij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охотиться.html>охо́титься</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oxótitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">охотнее</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oxotneje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охотно.html>охо́тно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oxótno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неохота.html>неохо́та</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neoxóta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Сame into use as taboo avoidance of an earlier word <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лов.html>лов</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lov</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; derived from Etymology 1.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oxóta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hunt, hunting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драма.html>дра́ма</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́те</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dráma na <b>oxóte</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Drama on the hunt  (Russian title of the novel "The Shooting Party")</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>shooting, game shooting, fowling</li>
<li>chase</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:хота.html>хо́т</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>ни́к</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:охотничий.html>охо́тничий</a> (5780)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охотник.html>охо́тник</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oxótnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охотничий.html>охо́тничий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oxótničij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>hunting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:охотничий.html>охо́тничье</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ружье.html>ружьё</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oxótničʹje</b> ružʹjó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shotgun; sporting gun; fowling-piece</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:охотничий.html>охо́тничья</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oxótničʹja</b> sobáka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hunting dog; gundog; hound</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:охотничий.html>охо́тничий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:домик.html>до́мик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oxótničij</b> dómik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shooting box/lodge</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:охотничий.html>охо́тничий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сезон.html>сезо́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oxótničij</b> sezón</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hunting season; shooting season</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:охотничий.html>охо́тничий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нож.html>нож</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oxótničij</b> nož</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hunting knife</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:охотничий.html>охо́тничье</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:угодье.html>уго́дье</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oxótničʹje</b> ugódʹje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hunting ground; game habitat; shooting preserve</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>hunter's

***охранка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:охранка.html>охра́нка</a> (21921)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охрана.html>охра́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oxrána</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">guard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">abbreviation of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отделение.html>отделе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:охранение.html>охране́нию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:общественный.html>обще́ственной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:безопасность.html>безопа́сности</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядок.html>поря́дка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Otdelénije po oxranéniju obščéstvennoj bezopásnosti i porjádka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>.. Also called <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охранный.html>охра́нное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отделение.html>отделе́ние</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Oxránnoje otdelénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for short.
</p>

</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">охрани́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oxranítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***оценить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оценить.html>оцени́ть</a> (2496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ценить.html>цени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оценить.html>оцени́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ocenítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оценивать.html>оце́нивать</a></b>)
</p>

<li>to evaluate, to estimate</li></ol>

***оценка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оценка.html>оце́нка</a> (2522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оценить.html>оцени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ocenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оценка.html>оце́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">océnka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оценка.html>оце́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оценка.html>оце́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оценка.html>оце́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>valuation, appraisal, feedback</li>
<li>estimation, appreciation</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">school</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mark, grade (where 5 = A, 1 = F)</li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оцепенеть.html>оцепене́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ocepenétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цепенеть.html>цепене́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow torpid, to become rigid, to freeze
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оцепенеть.html>оцепене́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>стра́ха</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ocepenétʹ</b> ot stráxa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to freeze with fear</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оцепенение.html>оцепене́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ocepenénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оцепене́лый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ocepenélyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — оцепеневать, <a href = vnd.unilang:цепенеть.html>цепене́ть</a>.

***оцинковать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оцинковать.html>оцинкова́ть</a> (28101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">цинкова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cinkovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оцинковать.html>оцинкова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ocinkovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">цинкова́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оцинко́вывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to zinc, to galvanize with zinc, to electroplate with zinc</li></ol>
